Settings</a></nav><script>$(function() {
  $('.drawer-links a[data-section]').click(function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var section = $(this).data('section');
    if (window.__setDashboardSection) {
      window.__setDashboardSection(section);
    }
    $('#nav-drawer').removeClass('open');
    $('#nav-drawer-overlay').removeClass('open');
  });
});
// Header character lookup. When the dashboard React app is loaded, hand
// the value to it so the lookup happens in-place (SPA); otherwise fall
// back to a full POST to /character.
function dashboardHeaderSearch(formEl) {
  var val = (formEl.character.value || '').trim();
  if (!val) { return false; }
  if (window.__dashboardSearch) {
    window.__dashboardSearch(val);
    formEl.character.blur();
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}</script></div><style>.search-input:focus {
